-03- COMMAND-CHANGE RELICS
------------------------------------------------------------

============================================================
-04- COMMANDS
------------------------------------------------------------

Cure2
-------
Use the skill 'Cure 2'

FenrReg
-------
Use the combo Fenrir + Regen.

OveQuak
-------
Use the combo Overcast + Quake.

PumBolt
-------
Use the combo Pummel + Bolt Beam.

QuadraS
-------
Use the skill 'Quadra Slice'

R-Magic
-------
Use a random magic spell.
Equal chance of any of the following:
  Antdot, Bio, Bolt, Bserk, Demi, Dispel, Doom, Drain, Fire, Fire 2, Fire 3, Flare, Float, Haste, Haste2, Ice 3, Merton, Meteor, Mute, Osmose, Rasp, Regen, Rflect, Safe, Scan, Shell, Sleep, Slow, Stop, Ultima, Vanish, W Wind

R-Rare
-------
Use a random rare effect (Slots, Super Ball, non-Lore monster skill).
Equal chance of any of the following:
  Absolute 0, Acid Rain, Blaster, Blaze, Blizzard, Fire Ball, Fire Wall, Flare Star, Flash Rain, Gale Cut, Grav Bomb, H-Bomb, HyperDrive, Launcher, Lode Stone, Love Token, Magnitude8, Megazerk, Meteo, Mind Blast, Missile, Net, Overcast, Phantasm, R.Polarity, Raid, Revenger, Schiller, Shock Wave, Soul Out, Tentacle, WallChange

ShockWa
-------
Use the skill 'Shock Wave'
